<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвлекаться.html>отвлека́ться</a> (7965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлекать.html>отвлека́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvlekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлекаться.html>отвлека́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvlekátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлечься.html>отвле́чься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be distracted, to deflect/divert one's attention away</li>
<li>to digress
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлекаться.html>отвлека́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otvlekátʹsja</b> v stóronu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">be wandering</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to abstract oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлекать.html>отвлека́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvlekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлечь.html>отвле́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvléčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлечься.html>отвле́чься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvléčʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвлекаться.html>отвлека́ться</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвоёванный.html>отвоёванный</a> (18218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́д</a> (17104)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>withdrawal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаз</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>otvóda</b> glaz</i> ― <span class="e-translation">as a blind; as a decoy; as a diversionary move</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otvód</b> vojsk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">withdrawal of troops</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rejection, objection, challenge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кандидат.html>кандида́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ <b>otvód</b> kandidátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reject a candidate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заявить.html>заяви́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судья.html>судье́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zajavítʹ <b>otvód</b> sudʹjé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">challenge the judge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>allotment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвод.html>отво́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:участок.html>уча́стка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строительство.html>строи́тельство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otvód</b> učástka pod stroítelʹstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">siting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pipe bend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electricity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tap, tapping, bend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">naval</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spreader</li></ol>

***отводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отводить.html>отводи́ть</a> (6073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отводить.html>отводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвести.html>отвести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead away; to take / draw aside; to take away</li>
<li>to divert</li>
<li>to avert, to parry; to deflect; to draw off; to ward off</li>
<li>to allocate, to assign</li>
<li>to withdraw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отводить.html>отводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>войска́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этап.html>эта́па</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otvodítʹ</b> vojská v dva etápa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to withdraw troops in two stages</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:отводить.html>отводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>otvodítʹ</b> dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unburden one's heart, to pour out one's heart</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to recuse</li></ol>

***отвоевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвоевать.html>отвоева́ть</a> (18218)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевать.html>воева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vojevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвоевать.html>отвоева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvojevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвоевывать.html>отвоёвывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to win <i>(from)</i>, to win over, to win back <i>(from)</i></li>
<li>to fight <i>(for some time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:отвоевать.html>отвоева́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní tri goda <b>otvojeváli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">they fought for three years</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to finish [be through with] fighting</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>война́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vojná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йско</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vójsko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войсковой.html>войсково́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vojskovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ин</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vóin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воинский.html>во́инский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vóinskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***отвозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвозить.html>отвози́ть</a> (15882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвозить.html>отвози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвезти.html>отвезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take away (by vehicle), to drive away, to take (somebody or something by vehicle)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"><a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>.
</th>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отворачивать.html>отвора́чивать</a> (21572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отвороти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отворачивать.html>отвора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвернуть.html>отверну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отвороти́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn aside, to turn away</li>
<li>to fold down, to turn down (e.g. a blanket)</li>
<li>to loosen, to remove (e.g. a stone from a fence)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отвороти́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otvorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in various meanings</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отвёртывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otvjórtyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отворачиваться.html>отвора́чиваться</a> (7541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отворачивать.html>отвора́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvoráčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отворачиваться.html>отвора́чиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvoráčivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвернуться.html>отверну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn aside, to turn away, to avert one's face/eyes</li>
<li>to break <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to turn away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to turn one's back</li>
<li>to come unscrewed</li>
<li>to bend back</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отворачивать.html>отвора́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvoráčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***отворить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отворить.html>отвори́ть</a> (8718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*otъvorìti</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-твори́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tvorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отворить.html>отвори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otvorítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отворять.html>отворя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to open (a door, a gate, or a window)</li></ol>
